TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">己二破<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">故但知果地融通。不了因心本具。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">己三示<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若尔。非但无情无性。有情亦无。何者。须约真如心说唯心。则成遮那有佛性。真常色说唯色。则成寂光有佛性。何关有情烦恼心无情生死色耶。具如金 中说。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]相宗之人立五性宗。一声闻性。二缘觉情。三阐提性。此三种人永不成佛。故曰定性二乘极恶阐提不成佛。惟许不定性菩萨性成佛。谓之三无二有。性宗虽胜于相。又言无情惟许有法性。无有佛性。故云墙壁瓦砾不成佛。具如荆溪大师金刚 中说。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丁二谬破　二　戊一引他人谬破问<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">问。有人云。南岳天台。令依三谛之理修三止三观。教义虽最圆妙。然其趣入门户次第。亦只是高僧所修四禅八定诸禅行相。唯达摩所传顿同佛体。今此所明。何相反耶。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]此即圭峰禅师禅源诠都序语。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">戊二以今宗正旨答　五　己一斥彼谬破<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">答。良由他人见今家立第六识为所观阴境。乃谓权教所诠。观第九识。方同佛体。如斯指斥。谬之甚矣。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]圭峰言今家门户次第者。门户是指今宗初心所观之境即第六识心。次第是今家所历之位。此圭峰但据天台三种止观之一种。便尔谬破。不知今家有三种止观。一圆顿止观。即摩诃止观是也。二渐次止观。即禅波罗密是也。三不定止观。即六妙门禅是也。若依禅门。且如所云。圆顿止观。彼未梦见也。此三止观所观事境。皆依六识。今记文所答。一往约境而言。故以六识而破之也。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">己二示今正义<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">前虽已辨。今更评之。若论境者。唯尚近要。即以第六识心以为所观之境。知妙三识未尝暂离一见一思。虽唯一识。未尝不以三识为观。未尝不以三识为境。众生在迷。故唯尚近要。故止观道者即其近要而顿示之。盖知七八九三种妙识未尝暂离六识见思。如善求水者必即波以汲。不善者则离波以求。是故今家虽以六识而观。未尝不观乎三识也。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">己三反破他说　二　庚一破他<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若直以此心缘于佛界实相理者。如用藕丝悬山。徒增分别。绝念无由。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]佛界境胜。犹如须弥。现前六识。喻如藕丝。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">庚二显今<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">何者。此第六识既是见思熏起。能起忻厌分别。作善恶因。即是修恶。体此修恶即是性恶。是为能观观法。复是所显法门。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]此之六识。虽是修恶之极。以今家有微妙三观、体此修恶全性恶起、当体即是性恶。岂不即以此而为能观妙观。即以此而为所显法门。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">己四引祖诰证　二　庚一引<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">故荆溪云。忽都未闻性恶之名。安能信有性德之行。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">庚二释<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">以由修恶即性恶。故三观十乘。无惑可破。无理可显。方名无作妙行。乃至果上普现色身。垂形九界。游戏六道。全性恶起。得名无谋而应。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]修恶既即性恶。故无惑可破。修恶既即性恶。故无理可显。如此修之。方名无作妙行之妙因。方名无谋而应之妙果。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">己五复斥于彼<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若也翻恶为善。断恶证善。因中行成有作。果上作意神通。何异外道。如此称为顿同佛体。乃认鱼目作明珠。指山鸡为鸾凤。虽三尺童子。亦知其谬。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丙四以圆更示　四　丁一约善恶极论<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若以性恶对乎性善。约十界次第迭论者。六界为恶。二乘为善。八界为恶。菩萨为善。九界为恶。佛界为善。此之九一。乃是恶之际善之极。故今所辨。盖就极论。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]今家论十界善恶。有偏论极论。今以九界为恶佛界为善。乃就极论。莫不直指九界之人、若三恶、若三善、若二乘、若菩萨、所有修恶即是性恶、性恶融通见性成佛而已。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丁二以圆别对明<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">圆人性具善恶。故如君子不器。善恶俱能。体用不二。别人不具性恶。故如淳善人不能造恶。为无明所牵方能造恶也。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]君子不器文出论语。子曰君子不器。注曰器者各适其用、而不能相通、成德之士、体无不具、故用无不周、非特一才一艺而已。今之取喻。则以其君子能文能武、以并夫真如具善具恶、能随染净缘具造十法界。非如别教但中佛性、如淳善人、但能善而不能恶、被恶人逼勉强作恶也。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丁三引经论证成　二　戊一释论　二　己一正引论文<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">释论云。淫欲即是道。痴恚亦复然。如是三法中。具一切佛法。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">己二释修即性<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">淫欲痴恚。修恶也。具一切佛法。即性恶也。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">戊二法华　二　己一正引经文<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">又经曰。弹指散华低头合掌皆成佛。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">己二释修即性<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">弹指等。修善也。皆成佛道者。即性善也。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丁四以力用结归　二　戊一正明力用<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">夫如是。莫不咸使法界有情、复此本有自性而已矣。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]谓能如上约修性善恶而论。得悟乎此。则何有无情而不即佛。又何有有情修之而不成佛。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">戊二用之传心<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">故得山林之下。草泽之士。精究佛乘。弘宣圣化。或于师门耳提面命。见而知之。或于经疏研几索隐。闻而知之。见闻之闲。两心相照。玄领默契。名之为传。我心本具。不从他得。名为不传。心虽本具。点示方知。是为传此不传之妙。如印印心。是名心印。知此者名妙解。行此者名妙行。证此者名妙果。如此则能事毕矣。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">乙二明化他　三　丙一重明自行　二　丁一承上转下<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">如上所论。且在自行。未涉化他。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丁二释成自行　四　戊一初祖<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">何者。迦叶于譬说中一闻即悟。不假修持。具领五时施化。故曰说法据此故施开自在。遂蒙如来述成授记。故知迦叶传此心印。的在法华。闻譬者。妙解也。悟入者。妙果也。故曰今法王大宝自然而至。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">戊二余人<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">迦叶既尔。余可例然。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">戊三金口<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">金口既然。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">戊四今师<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">今师亦尔。北齐一披其文。朗然大悟。南岳九旬乃证。天台二七方克。故知从闻而思思修而证。根性不同。证有迟速。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丙二正明化他　二　丁一标通别<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若论化他。名为付托。亦名嘱累。仍有通别。通该四众。别在迦叶。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丁二释通别　二　戊一通该四众<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">如劝持读诵嘱累流通。乃在余深法中示教利喜。声闻则具有八千。菩萨则无量无数。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">戊二释别在初祖　二　己一总标<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">别则唯在迦叶。付嘱不局一处。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">已二别明　二　庚一明两处付嘱　二　辛一涅盘经<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">故涅盘中虽不在会。欲令四众咸知敬信有在。乃曰我今所有无上正法以付摩诃迦叶。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">辛二付法传<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">又付法传云。化缘将毕。垂当灭度。告大弟子摩诃迦叶。如我今者将般涅盘。以此深法用嘱累汝。汝当于后敬顺我意。广宣流布。无令断绝。若尔。经必有文。不尽度耳。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">庚二明佛有三意　三　辛一标<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">所以独付迦叶者。有三意故。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">辛二释<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">一者如来缘谢。迦叶缘兴。二者迦叶苦行。能令佛法久住。三者付于小果。化导易行。例如净明德佛付嘱一切众生喜见菩萨广令流布是也。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">辛三结<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">盖由缘不在彼。是以付托于斯。岂传佛心印独在迦叶、余皆不了耶。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丙三斥他不知<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">世人昧此。诬罔圣贤。妄生戏论。未能知此自行化他的传之旨也。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">甲三总结心印之妙　四　乙一正赞其妙　二　丙一法<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">鸣呼。是为一家古今绝唱佛祖正传。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">丙二喻<span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">但白雪阳春。唱高和寡耳。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">       <o:p>       &nbsp;      </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明ify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">         <o:p>         &nbsp;        </o:p> </span></span></b></p><b> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">乙二谦光自鄙<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">则幸逢嘉运。不辞鄙陋。辄凭纸墨。以广见闻。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">乙三效古流通<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">效法华若田若里。涅盘若树若石。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]若田若里者。法华经云。若城邑巷陌聚落田里。如其所闻。为父母宗亲善友知识。随力演说。若树若石者。涅盘经云。佛昔为婆罗门。于雪山修行。有罗刹唱云。诸行无常、是生灭法。闻已欲求全偈。罗刹饥渴必得肉血食之。乃肯为说。因得后半偈云。生灭灭已、寂灭为乐。遂遍书树石。乃以身施之也。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="COLOR: #333399;  mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">乙四为下强毒　二　丙一法<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">或生谤毁。庶几强毒。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p></o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">        <o:p>        &nbsp;       </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]强毒者。譬喻也。譬如色声香味触五尘中皆有毒。见之闻之嗅之尝之触之皆能致死。色如毒龙之目。见之即死。声如涂毒之鼓。闻之即亡。香如毒龙之气。嗅之即丧。味如砒霜鸩毒。尝之即伤。触如毒蛇之口。螫之即毙。经中多约声味以明。如云涂毒之鼓、闻其声者、随其势力、死有延速。置毒五味。亦复如是。此皆反喻。以佛之大法。喻之如毒。人得闻之。使无明生死断</span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><b><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">如兽渡河。岂敢顾于濡尾者也。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">         <o:p></o:p> </span></b></p><b> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">         <o:p>         &nbsp;        </o:p> </span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><b><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">[注]易曰。小狐吃济濡其尾厉。盖言狐之涉水。濡尾则不能济。岂敢顾于濡尾者。良以谤毁之人、亦与下强毒种子。遑恤其他。故曰如兽渡河岂敢顾于濡尾者也。足徵记主之意。但欲佛之心印传于天下万世。不顾人之谤毁也。所谓将此深心奉尘刹。虎溪大师其人欤。</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style=" mso-bidi-font-weight: bold">         <o:p></o:p> </span></p> </b></b></b></b></b></b>
